The Nokia 107 is a low range priced handset with a few basic features on the board. The device is aimed at the people who don't want to use complex smartphones. The device has a 1.8 inch QVGA TFT display with 65K colours support and a resolution of 160 x 128 pixels, which is good enough to make calls and read texts. The phone has 4 MB of RAM to carry out basic tasks on this feature phone. Nokia 107 has an alphanumeric keypad that is comfortable for typing and dialling numbers. It also has support for dual-SIM functionality with dual stand-by mode.. Nokia 107 does not feature any kind of camera. It has FM radio and also support microSD card slot so that you can store music files on the phone and listen to them on the go with the inbuilt music player. It has 32-bit polyphonic ringtones, which you can assign to the contacts.. The device has 2G network support but lacks either 3G or Wi-Fi. The phone does not have Bluetooth for transferring data. The device has a micro USB port that only works for charging. The device can store up to 500 contacts in the phonebook.. The Nokia 107 features a 1020 mAh (BL-5C) battery that gives up to 576 hours of stand-by time, 12 hours of talk-time and 35 hours of music playback. The device does not have internal storage but has a microSD card slot that supports up to 16 GB cards.. Please ask the question in above box. Does it have an auto call recording option?. With millions of users and more than 300,000 sellers, Snapdeal is the online shopping site for Internet users across the country, delivering to 6000+ cities and towns in India. Specs of Nokia 107 Dual SIM. Standby Up to 576 h, Talk Time Up to 12 h 40 min, Music Play Up to 35 h. 1.8 inches (~114 ppi pixel density). GSM 900 / 1800 - SIM 1 & SIM 2. 112.9 x 47.5 x 14.9 mm, 70.6 cc (4.44 x 1.87 x 0.59 in). Nokia 107 takes affordability to its peak. This phone measures 112.9 x 47.5 x 14.5 mm in dimensions and weighs 75.8 grams. It is based on GSM technology. Screen size of this phone is 1.8 inches and has a resolution of 128 x 160 pixels (114 ppi). The screen is of TFT type and can display up to 65K colors. It has 4 MB of working RAM. Storage space can be increased up to 16 GB with the help of micro SD, and can store up to 500 contacts. Additional features include Polyphonic ring tone, Vibration, Loudspeaker, 3.5 mm audio jack, FM radio, SMS, Games and Java support. Other features include playability of Digital clock, MP3 player, Calculator, Converter, Calendar, Expense manager. Powered by a 1020mAh battery, the Nokia 107 promises standby time up to 576 hours, talk time over 12 hours, and music play of 35 hours. This model is available in black, white and red colors. Among other super cheap and extremely large battery life phone in Philippines has another addition to its lineup in the form of Nokia 107. Sure, the days of smart phones are here, and almost everybody has one, but there are still some people who like the feel and joy of using a classic phone. Used mainly for the purpose of calling and sending SMS, these phones serve as an ideal backup device to those that already own a higher end phone or as a beginner's phone for those who are looking forward to buying a mobile phone for the first time.. Contrary to the beliefs of most people, there is actually a niche market for phones that are low cost and high on battery life. Nokia 107 happens to be one such phone that enjoys that credibility and has earned its place among hearts of thousands of Filipinos. Some of the reasons why this phone is popular are:. Battery life: The primary reason this phone is popular is because of its humongous battery life that can last for days. The 1020mAh works like a charm and supports up to 35 hours of music playback non-stop! Having a standby time of 576 hours, this phone serves as the ideal backup device for those using smart phones and is constantly on the move. This phone saves the day where smart phones fail.. Display: Equipped with a 1.8 inches color screen, this device can perfectly display texts, images and games. The color screen is a bonus because people who are on an extremely low budget would probably expect to get a black and white variant. There is no problem related to vision as this phone displays large icons and clear non-pixilated SMS texts.. Entertainment value: This phone is armed with a loudspeaker that can light up a party scene. No longer will you have to share headphone with your friends. Go out there and impress others with the sound of Nokia 107. Java support makes it easier to install various apps, provided you extended memory size than the default. Extending storage space will also allow you to carry a huge number of songs to be played at your disposal.. Utility: Features such as Calendar, converter, calculator, and expense manager can make your life a whole lot easier by simplifying daily tasks and aiding in quick decision making. Thus, it is not hard to understand that this phone has all that it takes to be a hit.. Some competitors of Nokia 107 are Nokia 108, Nokia 106, Nokia 220 and other phones of the same price range. Local Filipino brand Cherry Mobiles and My Phone also pose a threat with their lineup of affordable phones.. Even though this phone would have been better with a camera, it is in no way a device that ranks lower than the affordable, camera equipped ones. Judging by all the features and the extremely low price tag, the Nokia 107 is certainly a good phone option if you are in Philippines.. Reviews of Nokia 107 Dual SIM. User Review : 2 Reviews. Why my Nokia 107 Dual SIM Unlock Code is locked?. When you purchase a cell phone it is often offered at a discounted price by the cellular network. In return for this generosity they "lock" your Nokia 107 Dual SIM Unlock Code to their network, so that you can only use their network for making and receiving calls. This means that you cannot use the SIM card of another network, and if you try to do so the phone will display "Phone Restricted", “Contact Service Provider”, “Enter Unlock Code” or a similar message. A SIM card or Subscriber Identity Module is a portable memory chip used in GSM phones. The SIM Card allows users to change phones by simply removing the SIM Card from one cell phone and inserting it into another. The SIM holds personal identity information, cell phone number, phone book, text messages and other data. How does the remote unlocking work?. SmartGSM es una de las comunidades de habla hispana más grandes sobre teléfonos celulares. Fundado en el 2004, smartGSM cubre todas las noticias y novedades sobre telefonía móvil y provee características de teléfonos celulares, smartphones, tablets y wearables. smartGSM cuenta con una comunidad de usuarios que reflejan sus experiencias, opiniones y críticas sobre teléfonos celulares y tablets..
